   - The opponent's strategy might involve cycling through rock, paper, scissors, with a bias towards repeating paper and scissors.

   - The opponent might be using a strategy that involves playing scissors and paper more frequently than rock.

4. **Reward Analysis**:

   - The opponent might be using a strategy that cycles through rock, paper, and scissors, but with a higher frequency of scissors.
